    <div style="text-align: left; text-indent: 36pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-size: 10pt;">On August 21, 2020, T-Mobile US, Inc. (&#8220;<span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;">T-Mobile</span></span>&#8221;)




      provided information regarding tax reporting with respect to the subscription rights to purchase T-Mobile&#8217;s common stock, par value $0.00001 per share, that were issued on June 26, 2020 to T-Mobile&#8217;s stockholders as of 5:00 p.m., Eastern Time, on
      June 25, 2020.</div>

      Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended (the &#8220;<span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;">Exchange Act</span></span>&#8221;), or otherwise subject to the liabilities of that section, nor shall they be deemed

  <head>
    <title></title>

<body bgcolor="#ffffff" style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; text-align: left; color: #000000;">
  <font style="font-weight: bold; font-size: 10pt;"> </font>
  <div>
    <hr noshade="noshade" align="center" style="height: 4px; color: #000000; background-color: #000000; text-align: center; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; border: none;">
    <div style="text-align: right; font-size: 10pt;"><font style="font-weight: bold;">Exhibit 99.1<br>
      </font></div>
  </div>
  <font style="font-weight: bold; font-size: 10pt;"> </font>
  <div style="font-size: 10pt;"><br>
  </div>
  <div>
    <div style="text-align: center; font-family: 'Times New Roman',Times,serif; font-size: 10pt; font-weight: bold;">T-Mobile US, Inc. (TMUS)</div>
    <div style="text-align: center; font-family: 'Times New Roman',Times,serif; font-size: 10pt; font-weight: bold;">Tax Reporting of Subscription Rights to Purchase Shares of Common Stock</div>
    <div style="text-align: center; font-family: 'Times New Roman',Times,serif; font-size: 10pt; font-weight: bold;">that were Issued on June 26, 2020</div>
    <div style="font-size: 10pt;"><br>
    </div>
    <div style="text-align: left; font-family: 'Times New Roman',Times,serif; font-size: 10pt;">In connection with a monetization by a subsidiary of SoftBank Group Corp. (&#8220;SoftBank&#8221;) of a portion of its shareholdings in T-Mobile US, Inc. (&#8220;T-Mobile&#8221; or the
      &#8220;Company&#8221;), each shareholder of the Company&#8217;s common stock (the &#8220;Common Stock&#8221;) received a subscription right (the &#8220;right&#8221;) to purchase 0.05 shares of T-Mobile Common Stock for each full share of T-Mobile Common Stock that such shareholder owned as
      of 5:00 p.m. (E.T.) on June 25, 2020 (the &#8220;Record Date&#8221;).&#160; This means that each shareholder received a number of rights that entitled such shareholder to purchase 1 share of T-Mobile Common Stock for each 20 shares owned by such shareholder as of the
      Record Date.&#160; There was no charge to shareholders in connection with the distribution of the rights.&#160; If not exercised, the rights expired on July 27, 2020 at 5:00 p.m. (E.T.).&#160; The remainder of this document discusses the potential U.S. federal
      income tax consequences to United States persons of various outcomes associated with the rights.&#160; This document is not intended to replace or amend the Prospectus Supplement, dated June 23, 2020, which was filed with the Securities and Exchange
      Commission in connection with the rights offering and contains a discussion of &#8220;Material U.S. Federal Income Tax Considerations.&#8221;&#160; Recipients of the rights should consult their own tax advisors to discuss the tax consequences associated with their
      receipt, sale, exercise or expiration of the rights.</div>
    <div style="font-size: 10pt;"><br>
    </div>
    <div style="text-align: left; font-family: 'Times New Roman',Times,serif; font-size: 10pt;">The Company has determined the fair market value of each right to be $0.26 upon issuance.&#160; As described in the Prospectus Supplement, the Company and SoftBank
      agreed to treat the receipt of the rights as a taxable transaction by United States persons, resulting in the recognition of ordinary taxable income in the amount of the fair market value of the rights at issuance.&#160; Consistent with that view, the
      $0.26 per right fair market value is expected to be used for purposes of any required tax reporting (e.g., Form 1099-MISC) to recipients after the close of the 2020 calendar year in connection with the issuance of the rights.&#160; Once included in
      taxable income, the fair market value at issuance of $0.26 per right becomes the recipient&#8217;s tax basis in that right.&#160; Because the Company cannot dictate the tax reporting done by brokers in this instance, it is possible that tax basis information
      reported by certain brokers to recipients and the IRS will not match the $0.26 per right fair market value described herein.&#160; Care should be taken by recipients to ensure that their tax basis in the rights matches the amount included in taxable
      income.</div>
    <div style="font-size: 10pt;"><br>
    </div>
    <div style="text-align: left; font-family: 'Times New Roman',Times,serif; font-size: 10pt;">There were three possible outcomes for recipients of rights: (1) the rights could be exercised to purchase shares of Common Stock; (2) the rights could be sold;
      or (3) the rights could expire unexercised.&#160; The discussion and examples below assume the recipients of the rights recognized ordinary taxable income of $0.26 per right upon receipt of the rights.</div>
    <div style="font-size: 10pt;"><br>
    </div>
    <div style="text-align: left; font-family: 'Times New Roman',Times,serif; font-size: 10pt;"><u>Exercised</u></div>
    <div style="text-align: left; font-family: 'Times New Roman',Times,serif; font-size: 10pt;">If the right was exercised, there was no tax impact associated with the exercise of the right.&#160; The tax basis of each share of Common Stock purchased would be
      equal to the cash paid for the share ($103 per share), plus the total of the taxable value of the rights surrendered for the share upon exercise ($0.26/right, or $5.20 per share ($0.26 per right x 20 rights to purchase single share)).</div>
    <div id="DSPFPageBreakArea" style="clear: both; margin-top: 10pt; margin-bottom: 10pt;">
      <div id="DSPFPageBreak" style="page-break-after: always;">
        <hr noshade="noshade" style="border-width: 0px; clear: both; margin: 4px 0px; width: 100%; height: 2px; color: #000000; background-color: #000000;"></div>
    </div>
    <div style="text-align: left; font-family: 'Times New Roman',Times,serif; font-size: 10pt;"><u>Sold</u></div>
    <div style="text-align: left; font-family: 'Times New Roman',Times,serif; font-size: 10pt;">If the right was sold, the seller would generally recognize short-term capital gain or loss upon a sale of the right.&#160; The capital gain or loss would be equal
      to the difference between the proceeds from the sale of the right and the taxable value of the right ($0.26/right).</div>
    <div style="font-size: 10pt;"><br>
    </div>
    <div style="text-align: left; font-family: 'Times New Roman',Times,serif; font-size: 10pt;"><u>Expired</u></div>
    <div style="text-align: left; font-family: 'Times New Roman',Times,serif; font-size: 10pt;">If the right was allowed to expire unexercised, the taxable value of the right ($0.26/right) would generally be recognized as a short-term capital loss upon
      expiration.</div>
    <div style="font-size: 10pt;"><br>
    </div>
    <div style="text-align: left; font-family: 'Times New Roman',Times,serif; font-size: 10pt; font-weight: bold;"><u>Examples</u></div>
    <div style="text-align: left; font-family: 'Times New Roman',Times,serif; font-size: 10pt; font-weight: bold;"><u> <br>
      </u></div>
    <div style="text-align: left; font-family: 'Times New Roman',Times,serif; font-size: 10pt;">Facts:&#160; Joe owns 5,000 shares of T-Mobile Common Stock.&#160; On June 26, 2020, he receives 5,000 rights, which entitle him to purchase an additional 250 shares of
      T-Mobile Common Stock at a price of $103 per share.&#160; Joe recognizes $1,300.00 of taxable income upon receipt of the rights ($0.26 per right x 5,000 rights received).</div>
    <div style="text-align: left;"><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif;"> </font><font style="font-size: 10pt;"><br>
      </font></div>
    <table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0" style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; width: 100%; border-collapse: collapse; text-align: left; color: #000000;" id="z6fd6e2f7985c4d14a09e7c241a181127">

        <tr>
          <td colspan="2" style="border-left: 2px solid rgb(0, 0, 0); border-right: medium none rgb(0, 0, 0); border-top: 2px solid rgb(0, 0, 0); vertical-align: bottom; white-space: nowrap; font-size: 10pt;">
            <div style="text-align: left; font-family: 'Times New Roman',Times,serif; font-weight: bold;"> <br>
            </div>

e.removeAttribute('id');a.parentNode.appendChild(e)}}
if(e)e.style.display='block';Show.LastAR=e};Show.hideAR=function(){Show.LastAR.style.display='none'};Show.toggleNext=function(a){var e=a;while(e.nodeName!='DIV')e=e.nextSibling;if(!e.style){}else if(!e.style.display){}else{var d,p_;if(e.style.display=='none'){d='block';p='-'}else{d='none';p='+'}
e.style.display=d;if(a.textContent){a.textContent=p+a.textContent.substring(1)}else{a.innerText=p+a.innerText.substring(1)}}}
